# Nailgun

# Description __

A construction tool turned deadly. Effective against lightly armored enemies at extremely close ranges. The nails it uses as ammunition can be crafted from metal fragments.

Page views: 5,917  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Python Revolver](/rust/item/pistol.python)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/pistol.python)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/pistol.python~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/pistol.python~history)



# Python Revolver

# Description __

A highly powered, highly accurate six-shooter that is effective at short and even long ranges with a steady hand.

# Python Revolver __

* * *

The Python Revolver is a powerful handgun in Rust that is capable of dealing significant damage at close range. It can be loaded with up to 6 rounds of pistol ammo and is a popular choice among players for its accuracy and stopping power.

## Attachment Compatibility __

* * *

The Python Revolver is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Boost
    * Silencer
    * Muzzle Brake
    * Flash Hider
  * Sight: 
    * Holosight
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * 16x Zoom Scope
    * 4x Zoom Scope
    * 2x Zoom Scope
    * Laser Sight



## Damage __

* * *

The Python Revolver deals 45 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 200.

## Obtaining the Python Revolver __

* * *

The Python Revolver can be obtained from airdrops or by purchasing it from the Bandit Camp for 500 scrap.

## Craftable __

* * *

No, the Python Revolver is not craftable.

  * [ __History](/rust/item/pistol.revolver~history)



# Revolver

# Description __

_A shoddy eight-shooter._

The Revolver is a low-powered yet easily obtainable firearm, requiring few resources and craftable at a [Work Bench Level 1](workbench1). Due to its poor damage & cheap cost, it is best used as your first handgun temporarily throughout your early progression; aided by the fact it fires equally basic [Pistol Bullets](ammo.pistol).

## Crafting Costs __

  * 125 [Metal Fragments](metal.fragments)
  * 25 [Cloth](cloth)
  * 1 [Metal Pipe](metalpipe)



# Statistics __

  * Base Damage: **35**
  * Semi Automatic: **~5.5RPS**
  * Magazine Capacity: **8**



Although the Revolver uses a traditional revolving cylinder design, it _cannot_ be fractionally reloaded (akin to the [Bolt Action Rifle](rifle.bolt)) and must instead be reloaded all at once - in an identical fashion to pistols utilizing ordinary ammunition clips.

Page views: 8,762  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Semi-Automatic Pistol

# Description __

A semi-automatic pistol, fires rapidly and with good accuracy.

Page views: 6,530  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Pitchfork

# Description __

A 3 pronged pitchfork. Extremely easy to hit targets with.

Page views: 6,002  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Large Planter Box](/rust/item/planter.large)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/planter.large)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/planter.large~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/planter.large~history)



# Large Planter Box

# Description __

A large planter with enough room to plant 9 seeds.

Seeds placed in a planter grow faster as they would normally in the wild. When explosed to a light source they'll grow at a further additional rate.

Regularly watering your plants in the planter with fresh water will significantly increase their yield.

When a plant has reached maturity you can take clipping which copy the genetics of the plant to make clones.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x200 Wood
  * x2 Tarp



## Recycling Output __

  * x100 Wood
  * x1 Tarp



Page views: 5,901

[Home](/rust/) / [Small Planter Box](/rust/item/planter.small)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/planter.small)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/planter.small~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/planter.small~history)



# Small Planter Box

# Description __

A small planter with enough room to plant 3 seeds.

Seeds placed in a planter grow faster as they would normally in the wild. When explosed to a light source they'll grow at a further additional rate.

Regularly watering your plants in the planter with fresh water will significantly increase their yield.

When a plant has reached maturity you can take clipping which copy the genetics of the plant to make clones.

Page views: 3,096  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Pumpkin

# Description __

An edible vegetable that can also be worn as a hat. Eating it provides a small boost to health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 4,392  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Pumpkin Bucket

# Description __

A pumpkin basket to help you collect candy much faster during Trick or Treat events with left click. Use right click to throw candy

Page views: 3,578  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Research Table

# Description __

You can use this table to learn how to permanently craft items you have found in exchange for scrap.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x200 Metal Fragments
  * x20 Scrap



## Recycling Output __

  * x100 Metal Fragments

# RF Transmitter

# Description __

A hand held RF signal broadcaster. Left click to broadcast. Configurable with right mouse.

Page views: 8,752  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# RF Pager

# Description __

An RF Pager. An audible tone will be produced when a signal is picked up on the listening frequency. Can be set to silent mode.

Page views: 10,913  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/rifle.ak~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/rifle.ak~history)



# Assault Rifle

# Description __

_High Damage machine rifle_   
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# Infomation __

The Assault Rifle is an accurate, powerful, and fully automatic rifle that fires [5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle). rounds. It has a moderate rate of fire which allows for proficiency at close to medium range. Strong recoil makes it more difficult to fire in full-auto at long range, but experienced users may be able to control it more effectively. The Assault Rifle is generally used as an end-game multipurpose weapon, able to take fights at any range.

# Stats __

  * Damage: **50**
  * Accuracy: **4**
  * Recoil: **36.4**
  * Fire Rate: **450**
  * Range: **188**



# Ammo __

  * **30x** [5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle).
  * **30x** [HV 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.hv)
  * **30x** [Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.explosive)
  * **30x** [Incendiary 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.incendiary)



# Researching __

  * **1625x** [Scrap](scrap) to go thru the tech tree in a [Work Bench Level 3](workbench3)
  * **500x** [Scrap](scrap) at the [Research Table](research.table)



# Crafting __

  * **50x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)
  * **200x** [Wood](wood)
  * **1x** [Rifle Body](riflebody)
  * **4x** [Metal Spring](metalspring)



# Recycle __

  * **25x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)
  * **100x** [Wood](wood)
  * **2x** [Metal Spring](metalspring)
  * **1x50%** [Rifle Body](riflebody)



# Repair __

  * **13x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)
  * **40x** [Wood](wood)



# Loot __

  * **20%** Oil Rig Locked Crate
  * **20%** Locked Crate
  * **4%** Elite Tier Crate
  * **3%** Underwater Lab Elite Crate
  * **1%** Helicopter Crate
  * **1%** Heavy Scientist
  * **1%** APC Crate

  * [ __View](/rust/item/rifle.bolt)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/rifle.bolt~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/rifle.bolt~history)



# Bolt Action Rifle

# Description __

_A high powered, highly accurate rifle._   
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# Infomation __

The Bolt Action Rifle is a powerful late game rifle that offers high accuracy and high damage at the cost of speed. Having the most damage and least spread of any weapon, it is often used as a designated sniper rifle, and is commonly fitted with a scope to increase the sight range for the user. Its slow rate of fire greatly limits its use in close quarters combat, and its limited capacity forces users to take shots very carefully. Having a very fast bullet velocity, users need not lead targets or compensate for gravity as much as with other weapons firing a slower bullet.

# Stats __

  * Damage: **80**
  * Accuracy: **2**
  * Recoil: **7.0**
  * Fire Rate: **35**
  * Range: **574**



# Ammo __

  * **4x** [5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle).
  * **4x** [HV 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.hv)
  * **4x** [Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.explosive)
  * **4x** [Incendiary 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.incendiary)



# Researching __

  * **2500x** [Scrap](scrap) to go thru the tech tree in a [Work Bench Level 3](workbench3)
  * **500x** [Scrap](scrap) at the [Research Table](research.table)



# Crafting __

  * **20x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)
  * **1x** [Rifle Body](riflebody)
  * **3x** [Metal Pipe](metalpipe)
  * **1x** [Metal Spring](metalspring)



# Recycle __

  * **10x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)
  * **1x50%** [Rifle Body](riflebody)
  * **2x** [Metal Pipe](metalpipe)
  * **1x50%** [Metal Spring](metalspring)



# Repair __

  * **7x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)



# Loot __

  * **3%** Elite Tier Crate

  * [ __History](/rust/item/rifle.l96~history)



# L96 Rifle

# Description __

_A military issue high powered rifle._

The L96 Rifle is an end-game rifle featuring extremely accurate & long range capability. It fires [556 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle) and can generally be considered a direct upgrade from the [Bolt Action Rifle](rifle.bolt), with a single major drawback of instead being military quality - ultimately rendering it uncraftable by players.

## Obtaining __

Lootable Source | Chance | Condition  
---|---|---  
APC Crate | 8% | 100%  
Oil Rig Locked Crate | 3% | 100%  
Locked Crate | 3% | 100%  
Helicopter Crate | 0.3% | 100%  
Heavy Scientist | 0.2% | 100%  
Underwater Lab Elite Crate | 0.2% | 1-5%  
Elite Tier Crate | 0.2% | 1-5%  
  
# Statistics __

  * Base Damage: **80**
  * Single Shot: **Not Automatic**
  * Magazine Capacity: **5**



Although the L96 Rifle is military-grade, it offers no additional base damage over the Bolt Action Rifle.

A majorly beneficial (yet often undocumented) aspect of this rifle is the extremely high velocity it applies to fired bullets; requiring almost no leading of shots whatsoever. When paired with [HV 556 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.hv), it is comparable to wielding a [hitscan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hitscan) weapon (at ranges before bullet drop-off occurs).

Page views: 24,629  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __View](/rust/item/rifle.lr300)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/rifle.lr300~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/rifle.lr300~history)



# LR-300 Assault Rifle

# Description __

A high-powered assault rifle that deals less damage but has more manageable recoil than it's craft-able counterpart.

This is a military grade weapon, meaning it is not learn-able or craft-able and must be bought or found. It can be found rarely in locked crates, supply drops, heli crates, elite crates, and on the bodies of heavy scientist. The LR-300 is for sale at the bandit camp for 500 scrap.

  
  


# General Information __

The LR-300 is a military-grade weapon, meaning it is not learnable or craftable and must be bought or found. It can be found rarely in locked crates, supply drops, heli crates, elite crates, and on the bodies of heavy scientists. It can also be purchased at the Bandit Camp for 500 Scrap.

The LR-300 Assault Rifle has a moderate rate of fire and can be loaded with 30 rounds of 5.56 ammunition. It is compatible with a range of attachments, including scopes, muzzle attachments, and magazines.

## Damage and Durability __

The LR-300 deals 35 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 150.

## Attachment Compatibility __

The LR-300 is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Brake
    * Silencer
    * Flash Hider
  * Sight: 
    * Holosight
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * 16x Zoom Scope
    * 4x Zoom Scope
    * 2x Zoom Scope
    * Laser Sight
  * Magazine: 
    * 30-Round Magazine



The LR-300 Assault Rifle is a rare and powerful weapon in Rust that is sought after by players for its manageable recoil and compatibility with a range of attachments. While it may deal less damage than other assault rifles, its versatility and ease of use make it a formidable weapon in the right hands.

# M39 Rifle

# Description __

An un-craftable very accurate military-grade semi automatic rifle.

  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

The M39 Rifle is an uncraftable, military-grade, semi-automatic rifle in Rust known for its high accuracy and long-range capabilities.

The M39 Rifle is a powerful and versatile weapon that can be found in locked crates, heli crashes, and as a rare drop from elite crates. It is a semi-automatic rifle that fires 5.56 ammunition and can hold 8 rounds in a magazine.

The M39 Rifle is known for its high accuracy and long-range capabilities, making it an ideal choice for players who prefer to engage targets from a distance. It also has a relatively fast firing rate, which allows for quick follow-up shots.

## Attachment Compatibility __

* * *

The M39 Rifle is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Brake
    * Silencer
    * Flash Hider
  * Sight: 
    * Holosight
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * 16x Zoom Scope
    * 4x Zoom Scope
    * 2x Zoom Scope
    * Laser Sight
  * Magazine: 
    * 8-Round Magazine



## Damage __

* * *

The M39 Rifle deals 45 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 200.

## Obtaining the M39 Rifle __

* * *

The M39 Rifle can be obtained in the following ways:

  * Locked crates: Locked crates can be found in the game world and require a Supply Signal to call in an airdrop.
  * Heli crashes: Helicopter crashes occur randomly around the game world and contain a variety of loot, including the M39 Rifle.
  * Elite crates: Elite crates are found in the Launch Site, Military Tunnels, and other high-level areas.



As an uncraftable item, the M39 Rifle is highly prized among Rust players due to its accuracy and long-range capabilities. Whether you're a fan of long-range engagements or simply want a powerful and versatile weapon, the M39 Rifle is a solid choice that won't disappoint.

# Semi-Automatic Rifle

# Description __

An accurate semi-automatic rifle that is effective at medium-long ranges. The weapon of choice for midgame PvP battles.

Page views: 7,777  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Rifle Body

# Description __

The firing mechanism of a rifle. Used in construction of a weapon that can fire 5.56 ammo fully automatic.

Page views: 3,968  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Riot Helmet

# Description __

A makeshift riot Helmet. Great at deflecting melee attacks.

Page views: 2,942  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Roadsign Gloves

# Description __

Gloves made out of metal offers a good amount of protection to the upper body.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 10 %  
Melee | 15 %  
Bite | 10 %  
Cold | -8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Item does not stack and its despawn time is 5 min.

Page views: 5,702  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Road Sign Jacket

# Description __

A shoddy piece of body armor made from roadsigns.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 20 %  
Melee | 20 %  
Bite | 10 %  
Cold | -8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Item does not stack and its despawn time is 20 min.

Page views: 3,989  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/roadsign.kilt~history)



# Road Sign Kilt

# Description __

A shoddy piece of leg armor made from roadsigns.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 20 %  
Melee | 20 %  
Bite | 10 %  
Cold | -8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Item does not stack and its despawn time is 20 min.

Page views: 3,464  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Rock

# Description __

A Rock. The most basic melee weapon and gathering tool.

Page views: 5,470  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/rug~history)



# Rug

# Description __

A decorative rug that can be placed on walls, floors, and ceilings. Provides comfort when in close proximity. Comfort increases by a unit of 50 it does not stack.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x25 Cloth



## Recycling Output __

  * x13 Cloth
